# Comments for Question 4, LLM=Claude Opus 4 (no reasoning)

== Grader: Claude 3.7 Sonnet ==
  * grade_story_103.txt (grade=9.4)
    The story achieves exceptional emotional impact through layered symbolism (the mirror reflecting both literal images and moral truths). The central impossible choice reappears in multiple forms, creating thematic coherence. The subtext about forgiveness transcending death gives the narrative philosophical weight. The ending delivers profound catharsis while maintaining emotional complexity. Literary craft shines in the precision of language and the effective use of objects as emotional vessels.

  * grade_story_1.txt (grade=7.0)
    The story effectively explores themes of transformation and fear as a gateway to understanding. The metaphor of unraveling knots as releasing spiritual wisdom works well. However, some of the more profound revelations are stated rather than shown, particularly in the final paragraphs, which diminishes their impact. The story would benefit from allowing readers to experience these realizations more organically.

  * grade_story_0.txt (grade=8.0)

The central tension—approaching what others fear—resolves into a moment of transformative connection. The lamp's symbolism works on multiple levels (illumination, beauty within utility, transparency). The ending achieves emotional resonance while implying far-reaching consequences beyond the immediate narrative, leaving readers with philosophical questions about intelligence and evolution.
